<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7e76e050-a30d-417c-8df7-592aaf33d8cd'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer7689399044866597749">For Prime-Werewolf Ember Stilwell, life has been far from normal. Decades ago, a vengeful Witch cursed her Pack, leaving the women of her line incapable of feeling love.   <span id="freeText7689399044866597749" style="display:none">For Prime-Werewolf Ember Stilwell, life has been far from normal. Decades ago, a vengeful Witch cursed her Pack, leaving the women of her line incapable of feeling love. When an organized group of immortal killers begin to stalk and capture wolves from her pack, she sets out on a path fraught with danger. Just when it seems the world as she knows it will be changed forever, she meets Collin, an Alpha Werewolf with a body built for sin. As her heart begins to heal, she comes to find that the demons of her past are not nearly as dangerous as the nightmares she will be forced to face in her future. Can finding her true love conquer all? Or will the ability to feel for the first time be overshadowed by losing everything else she holds dear?</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer515845246" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8005185466530950693">I received Ember's curse from the author as an ARC in exchange for an honest review. I have to say I haven't read anything paranormal in a very long time and typically not my first choice but as I started reading this one I was like..........................................................<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388386ra/748873.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Boy am I glad I took a chance on this one cause I liked, no that's not right, I really LOVED it! I was giddy while reading it kinda nice getting away from what you normally read and branching out and believe me</span>
  <span id="freeText8005185466530950693" style="display:none">I received Ember's curse from the author as an ARC in exchange for an honest review. I have to say I haven't read anything paranormal in a very long time and typically not my first choice but as I started reading this one I was like..........................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388386ra/748873.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Boy am I glad I took a chance on this one cause I liked, no that's not right, I really LOVED it! I was giddy while reading it kinda nice getting away from what you normally read and branching out and believe me I'll continue to take chances with what I read cause when you do that you find some great books!<br><br>Ember's Curse is the story of well, Ember! She is a werewolf with part vampire- not sure how that worked at first, but trust me in the end it ALL made sense. Ember was bad arse and she had mad skills. Heck in the beginning of the book her mad skills were introduced against a couple of werewolf's in another pack that had a lesson to be learned and well Ember just happened to do a little of this.....................................<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405245ra/789177.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>There was cursed placed on Ember's family many centuries ago by a witch which essentially left Ember incapable of feeling lust and love until she met "THE ONE". Ember's pack leader, Alpha, was her cousin Tommy and his ever so lovely wife, Sylvia- NOT! Sylvia will make you want to do this to her............................................................<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401282ra/778690.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It seems that Ember is always in "trouble" with Tommy which Slyvia feeds off of but she also feeds of her "power" since Tommy is her mate. Ember isn't out there all alone though never fear she has two very good friends. Nathan another werewolf who believe me ladies we will WANT to know more about him and her kick-arse vampire friend and roommate Harper! Oh Harper, how I loved her seriously that chick had no filter! It was quite amusing.<br><br>Well some big time stuff goes down, no I can't tell you what, and Nathan calls in his cousin Collin who is the Alpha male of Nathans pack. Ember first lays eyes on Collin and it was.......................<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406577ra/793450.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Speechless completely speechless as their eyes met and every thing else fades away BAM she found her man! Collin, fanning myself, well he was sex on legs ~ oh speaking of that yep when they first connected well let's just say they connect. If I was there and laid eyes on Collin I would of ..............................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/635999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Collin could be my Alpha, yes sirrrrreeeeee, oh but we aren't talking about me. There's a little hitch to this plan as we all knows nothing comes easily :) When you read the book you will find out what that hitch was!<br><br>I flew through this book ~ read it in one evening I loved it that much. We know I never, ever, give spoilers in my reviews but I can give you a few hints of what this book had. It had some..........................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406577ra/793451.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and....................................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406577ra/793452.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>yes two killer chicks ~ yep haters could hate but those girls had mad skills. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406577ra/793453.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>and of course..........................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406577ra/793454.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>yes a few vampires there to help and well complicate things and by the end I was..............................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/459304.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was like oh yes! This was a 5 +++ paranormal read for me. Outside my normal genre but it had everything I loved in a book. A kick arse female, a strong alpha male, hot sex and a lot of drama.<br><br>I recommend Ember's Curse the first book in the Prime Wolf series. I can't wait to see where this series goes and what happens with Nathan and Harper! There's many more in this book you will be introduced to but I have to pay homage to Ember since this is her book.<br><br>Gena THANK YOU! I loved this book and will eagerly await your next book.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16300325.Ember_s_Curse__Prime_Wolf_1_" title="Ember's Curse (Prime Wolf 1) by Gena D. Lutz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1355097718s/16300325.jpg" alt="Ember's Curse (Prime Wolf 1) by Gena D. Lutz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6653864.Gena_D__Lutz" title="Gena D. Lutz" rel="nofollow noopener">Gena D. Lutz</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9439374496654355932">I was fortunate enough to receive Ember's Curse as an ARC. Thank you Gena for the wonderful opportunity!! <br/><br/>Gena weaves us a wonderful tale of werewolves, vampires, hybrids, and so many more magical creatures that is very unique to the paranormal world! Ember is a dominant alpha she-wolf going through the motions until she finds her prime mate; her heart mate. She's a very strong female which is refreshing! <br/> Collin is the oh so yummy leader of the Adelphi pack, the protectors and law enforcers of </span>
  <span id="freeText9439374496654355932" style="display:none">I was fortunate enough to receive Ember's Curse as an ARC. Thank you Gena for the wonderful opportunity!! <br /><br />Gena weaves us a wonderful tale of werewolves, vampires, hybrids, and so many more magical creatures that is very unique to the paranormal world! Ember is a dominant alpha she-wolf going through the motions until she finds her prime mate; her heart mate. She's a very strong female which is refreshing! <br /> Collin is the oh so yummy leader of the Adelphi pack, the protectors and law enforcers of the supernatural world. You can think of Collin as the King of his kind. <br />I won't get into the story so as not to accidentally post spoilers but I will say that this is an amazing book! I wasn't sure what to expect before reading it but what I found was amazing! It's a unique story all it's own. Not your typical werewolf/vampire novel. But if you love either of those then you definitely need to read this!! You won't be disappointed!! Though you may be a little jealous of Ember once her and Collin consummate their relationship! Hott!! I just love alpha males! ;-) <br />Alright make sure you add this to your tbr list and buy it when it's released! I wish I could give it more than 5 Stars!! It's just that good!!<br />Gena I look forward to your future work!! I am now a huge fan!!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/476227395?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Olson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Olson" href="/user/show/9090653-rachel-olson">Rachel Olson</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer476227395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6486055921330219197">Ember's Curse is absolutely enthralling! The voice of Ember is so easy to read, you feel like you're taking an adventure...in her shoes!<br/><br/>I love the paranormal ideas behind Ember's Curse. There are so many of the loved, traditional creatures that have been created throughout history, but Gena has added her own personal touch to the concept of their existence. There's enough intriguing detail provided in the explanation of their makeup to be captivating without breaking the threshold into overpower</span>
  <span id="freeText6486055921330219197" style="display:none">Ember's Curse is absolutely enthralling! The voice of Ember is so easy to read, you feel like you're taking an adventure...in her shoes!<br /><br />I love the paranormal ideas behind Ember's Curse. There are so many of the loved, traditional creatures that have been created throughout history, but Gena has added her own personal touch to the concept of their existence. There's enough intriguing detail provided in the explanation of their makeup to be captivating without breaking the threshold into overpowering. Gena manages a beautiful balance in this story, drawing pictures with her words that help you "watch" the story unfold, all the while gripping the edge of your seat with a white knuckled grip. I laughed, sometimes hysterically; I cried, both in sadness and with joy. I cursed right alongside Ember and her mates, and mentally high-fived her countless times. <br /><br />Ember's Curse is a breath of fresh air, brimming with action, love, mystery, and suspense. Don't forget the pinch of comedy. With realistic personalities in a world only found in a good book, Ember's Curse will not disappoint.<br /><br />A special thanks to Gena for allowing me the opportunity to traipse about in her mind through this story. It was a grand pleasure to share in this little piece of her exposed soul.<br /><br />~Rachel A Olson, ParaSuperNormalism, Author</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7048595622661224357">This book has the makings of a very good series. It has all the things that I love in a paranormal/romance book. All kinds of sexy alpha males and kick butt women who take no crap. I LOVED this book pretty much from start to finish. Ember is kick butt awesome and let me tell you Collin was a hot, sexy, make you fall on the floor panting Alpha male. I am quite sure that future books (as I am sure this has to be a series) will only get better and better. There are so many stories left to tell. I absolutely cannot wait and sincerely hope there is many more books to come!!For Prime-Werewolf Ember Stilwell, life has been far from normal. <br />Decades ago, a vengeful Witch cursed her Pack, leaving the women of her line incapable of feeling love. When an organized group of immortal killers begin to stalk and capture wolves from her pack, she sets out on a path fraught with danger. Just when it seems the world as she knows it will be changed forever, she meets Collin, an Alpha Werewolf with a body built for sin. As her heart begins to heal, she comes to find that the demons of her past are not nearly as dangerous as the nightmares she will be forced to face in her future. Can finding her true love conquer all? Or will the ability to feel for the first time be overshadowed by losing everything else she holds dear?</span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781481275989" href="/book/show/22375319-ember-s-curse">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2583330-b?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2583330-b?shelf=suspense-mystery">suspense-mystery</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479605329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4486322899375592756">I have the pictures that the author used for inspiration posted on my blog <a href='http://wp.me/2wO9O' rel='nofollow noopener'>Momma's Books</a><br/><br/>So I have not read a paranormal book in a while so when I got an email from the author asking if I would read her book and do an honest review I was flattered as well as excited because well I did miss paranormal and just have been putting it off. After she sent me the book and I got into reading it I will have to say that this book reminded me as to why it was that I loved paranormal to begin with. Action ri</span>
  <span id="freeText4486322899375592756" style="display:none">I have the pictures that the author used for inspiration posted on my blog <a href="http://wp.me/2wO9O" rel="nofollow noopener">Momma's Books</a><br /><br />So I have not read a paranormal book in a while so when I got an email from the author asking if I would read her book and do an honest review I was flattered as well as excited because well I did miss paranormal and just have been putting it off. After she sent me the book and I got into reading it I will have to say that this book reminded me as to why it was that I loved paranormal to begin with. Action right from the get go. I have read some books where there is a mix of vampires and werewolves, witches and nymphs but this was the first that I had read that had a mix a 'hybrid'. I was sucked in right from the get go and couldn't put it down I wanted to know more and more and more. I had just forgotten how good paranormal was, and Gena Lutz writes it well!! I am so glad that she got a hold of me to read this because I loved it! I will recommend it to my friends who like paranormal books as well. <br /><br />There were so many twists and turns and so much action as well as hotness and well it just had everything! I absolutely love Ember and her best friend Harper they crack me up when they are together. There is just the perfect mix of romance, love, fighting and action, humor, and suspense. I don't want to give away too much about the book so doing this review is a little on the harder side because my favorite parts that I want to talk about would give away something. :( <br /><br />Instantly I loved Collin I mean who wouldn't? he is hot and ALL alpha! and then Nathan.. he is just the sweetest! but when you get the 'three stooges' together (Ember, Harper &amp; Nathan) you will laugh from time to time that is for sure! Harper is the no bs kind of girl and tells it like it is which always makes for fun times! :) <br /><br />If you are looking for a great paranormal to read then this is it! I am looking forward to the second book in the series! I loved the ending but was left wondering about a few things and was so happy to find out that there will be more! There is enough in here to satisfy anyone who enjoys paranormal without being to cheesy that is honestly what I get worried about when reading a new paranormal novel! <br /><br />So to sum up:<br /><br />Great action<br />Great love/romance<br />Good steam<br />Will make you giggle<br />Will pull your heart strings (for me it did when we got to know Dane)<br />Good suspense (kept me in suspenders)<br />Twists and turns<br />Non cheesy</span>

  <span id="freeText6143503143242859103" style="display:none">Imagine yourself being told that you will never be able to feel love due to a horrible curse only to be told you are to be married to someone you have never even met!<br /><br />As you try to accept that fate, which seems worse than death, you slam face to face with an amazing desire and love for one it seems was destined to be your lifemate?<br /><br />Sound like a disaster? Well this book threads you through the needle bit by bit as events unfold all around you that could change not only your fate but that of an entire species. <br /><br />This book would NOT allow me to set it down. I swear it was calling to me to read just one more page which resulted in it being read in about a day and what an amazing day.<br /><br />I was lost in the adventure, excitement, love, death, terror and there was even a sprinkling of humour thrown into the mix to make this a fantastic read.<br /><br />So go ahead and open the first page then hold on to your seat and get ready for a wild ride.<br /><br />Five stars well deserved and an amazing beginning to what I'm sure will be one awesome series.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer511726415" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5831538122448592222">Ember's curse is quite the exciting romance. Ember has been cursed to never feel love until she finds her one and only true mate. The chances of that happening anytime soon are pretty small. But when Collin walks into her life to help investigate werewolf slaying and kidnappings, all bets are off and she can only hope she survives long enough to figure out what the hell is happening to her.<br/><br/>One of my favorite parts of this book was that it wasn't just werewolves vs vampires vs witches vs human. E</span>
  <span id="freeText5831538122448592222" style="display:none">Ember's curse is quite the exciting romance. Ember has been cursed to never feel love until she finds her one and only true mate. The chances of that happening anytime soon are pretty small. But when Collin walks into her life to help investigate werewolf slaying and kidnappings, all bets are off and she can only hope she survives long enough to figure out what the hell is happening to her.<br /><br />One of my favorite parts of this book was that it wasn't just werewolves vs vampires vs witches vs human. Ember has friends from all those realms, and she has enemies from them all as well. The world was written in a way that supernatural types were just another part of life - some were good, some didn't care, and some were downright nasty.<br /><br />Ember and Collin have sparks flying all over the place, but don't really have time to do much about it at the moment (but they do sneak off a few times to make get some alone time in). The end of the book leaves with quite a cliffhanger - and a possible second romantic couple. With some things tied up nice and pretty with a ribbon and others running out of control, it was the perfect set up for a second book that I can't wait to read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5831538122448592222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Enter Ember Stilwell, a prime werewolf who benefits from both sides of the yin yang of paranormal creatures. Descended from a long line of primes, it is a wonder that Ember is </span>
  <span id="freeText13091222220487338500" style="display:none"><b>Emberâ€™s Curse</b><br /><b>A Prime Wolf Novel</b><br /><i>By Gena D. Lutz, Crimson Moon (December 15, 2012)</i><br /><br />Vampires and werewolves: the much adored villains vs. the undisputed heroes of earth. Many a character has been birthed from the hyperactive imaginations of authors, but did you know it is possible to be both vampire and werewolf, in one body? Enter Ember Stilwell, a prime werewolf who benefits from both sides of the yin yang of paranormal creatures. Descended from a long line of primes, it is a wonder that Ember is content to bar tend and bounce at Haven, a tavern for the different local species, rather than forcibly take the Alpha position of her pack. Able to influence weaker creatures, shape-shift, and exude an unbelievable, Beta trumping strength, Ember seems to have it all, including the enviable ability to walk away from love affairs unscathed.<br /><br />That is, until a mixed pack of renegade werewolves and vampires begin hunting down and imprisoning members of Emberâ€™s pack. Enter the Adelphi in the form of Collin Hayes, a powerful Alpha werewolf hell bent on eliminating the dangerous characters that seem to follow Ember wherever she goes. Immediately, Ember and Collinâ€™s lives are gripped in a breakneck sleuthing operation that would make even Sherlockâ€™s head spin. Combine addictive, fast paced action scenes with bodice ripping, hot love scenes between the two powerful Alphas and you have a book that gets the blood pumping. <br /><br />Written in first person, Ember engages the reader with a firsthand experience of not just the crazy situations she stumbles into, but also the mixed emotions she struggles with. Lutz wastes no time introducing the primary love interest before tumbling lovers and friends into the grips of evil. The story progressed almost too quickly, too smoothly: from lusty mating to power hungry vamps; dominated Alphaâ€™s and abused wolves; all knitted up in an ending that finally releases the reader from the exhausting spell Lutz has crafted. Even while cinching up this dizzyingly fun novel, Lutz is opening the door to another, potentially more merciful sequel. Emberâ€™s Curse starts with a bang (ahem!) and rockets off, dragging all who love an adventure packed romance along for the wild ride. <br /><br /><i>Reviewed by H. Herzog, who is a workaholic, gamely tending to the duties of family, garden, writing and a satellite installation warehouse all while really looking forward to the next good book to fall into her lap.</i><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536987540" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17692054756843842214">Werewolves, Vamps and Hybrids, OH MY! and OHHHHHH YEAH! This debut novel from Ms Lutz has some of the paranormal aspects we have all come to know and love but then she takes it to a whole new level with her vivid imagination and amazing story telling ability! Ember is a Prime Werewolf whose family was cursed by a witch many generations ago making it impossible for the women in their line to experience love until they find their "heart mate". And if that wasn't enough, she is also part vampire! E</span>
  <span id="freeText17692054756843842214" style="display:none">Werewolves, Vamps and Hybrids, OH MY! and OHHHHHH YEAH! This debut novel from Ms Lutz has some of the paranormal aspects we have all come to know and love but then she takes it to a whole new level with her vivid imagination and amazing story telling ability! Ember is a Prime Werewolf whose family was cursed by a witch many generations ago making it impossible for the women in their line to experience love until they find their "heart mate". And if that wasn't enough, she is also part vampire! Ember embodies everything you want in an Alpha female, she is bold and brazen, take charge and strong, courageous and loyal and has a super sense of humor dashed with enough sarcasm to make you laugh right out loud with her. She also has an amazing heart and is super protective of her friends and pack mates. That beautiful heart is thrown wide open from the first moment she lays eyes on Collin, a hot as sin Alpha male leader of the Adelphi, the ruling body of all things supernatural. The attraction is immediate, explosive and HOT HOT HOT!<br /><br />Ember and Collin get very little time to explore all these new amazing feelings as they are thrown headlong into deceit, betrayal and bullets flying through the air! As if this wasn't enough, their new bond is giving them new powers and they have no idea when or where they will appear. And I almost forgot to mention they get to meet and make a pact with an incredibly powerful King and Queen of the Lore!<br /><br />Ms Lutz is an incredibly talented writer. She makes Ember's narrative feel so real that you can imagine yourself listening to a friend over coffee retelling what's been going on in her life! Her ability to make all of the amazing happenings seem like they are actually occurring is worth every second you take to read this book! You can "see" what is happening and feel yourself yelling at the bad guys, cringing when Ember, Collin or one of their group get hit, swooning when they are looking into each other's eyes and fanning yourself when the loving begins!!! It will be my pleasure to read anything Ms Lutz writes and I hope there is more to come from Ember, Collin and the rest of this amazing cast of characters!<br /><br />Review by I Love Vampire Novels<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/ilovevampirenovels">www.facebook.com/ilovevampirenovels</a></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4914712813546037461">When I was asked by Gena if I'd like to read and review Ember's Curse I couldn't get out a yes fast enough! While I do love my rock stars and bad boys I also LOVE paranormal (I always end up wishing stuff like that was real, I think it would be hot to be able to shift into a wolf, or have super vampy speed and never age) especially a good paranormal that grabs you from the starts which this one definitely did. I love that Gena gave us a nice mix of supernatural beings here; werewolves, vampires,</span>
  <span id="freeText4914712813546037461" style="display:none">When I was asked by Gena if I'd like to read and review Ember's Curse I couldn't get out a yes fast enough! While I do love my rock stars and bad boys I also LOVE paranormal (I always end up wishing stuff like that was real, I think it would be hot to be able to shift into a wolf, or have super vampy speed and never age) especially a good paranormal that grabs you from the starts which this one definitely did. I love that Gena gave us a nice mix of supernatural beings here; werewolves, vampires, witches, hybrids, Fae and I have to say she blended them into the story seamlessly! <br />Our main character Ember is awesome she's a take no shit from anyone, even her Alpha leader...which kinda explains why she's usually on his shit list but whatev he's douchey as is his power hungry alpha mate Sylvia...in one scene she's admiring her manicure and all I could hear is "get your lee press on nails outta my face" from the 2nd Chimpmunk's movie lol) and Collin our sexy Adelphi pack leader is an alpha that would have any woman sitting up and begging *swoooooonnnnn* and when these two meet for the first time make sure your sitting down because the sparks and fur start flying, but in a completely hot and sexy way ;-) the secondary characters are equally awesome (no one's putting these guys in a corner!) <br /><br />I gotta hand it to Gena, she really did a fan-freakin-tastic job of taking you along Ember's adventure to find out who's got it in for her pack; she's blended magic and all sorts of mystical elements perfectly! <br />I always find it hard to talk about paranormal stories because for some reason I'm always more paranoid about giving spoilers away than I am with other books and I truly hate to ruin this for anyone because it really is such a great book. In addition to awesome characters, there's action, and magic topped with hot steamy loving between Ember and Collin. If you're a paranormal fan I highly suggest you give Ember's Curse a read and if you haven't read this genre before, this book would be a great one to start with<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText11551097783964936920" style="display:none"> This book kept me up at the wee hours of the night because it insisted that I finish it! Yeah it's good enough to keep me up! That means I want to share it with you guys! I did a book spotlight and a giveaway on it not too long ago, but I hadn't the chance to read it until now! I loved it! Really! Mixing a vampire and a werewolf and a curse! Genius! Hahaha <br />Ember is a bad ass. She holds her own and can handle her load quite well. Even with the family curse of not "feeling" anything for anyone, she still manages to keep great friendships that get her through her existence in a pack with an alpha that makes you want to strangle his furry little behind! Thrown in a situation that brings danger to her and her friends she struggles to break free from all the evil around her, but will finding her soul mate and breaking free of the family curse solve her problems or make them worse? <br /> Strange things are happening to her body. Things that have never been explained and prophecies that she's never heard of! With sexy, sweet, HAWT Collin by her side I think these two can manage anything! Even being captured and shot at and chased...yeah this book is full of non stop action, full sexy scenes, characters with a bite (literally) and honestly you're going to want to pick this up! We are tossed into the life of Ember and all the issues thrown her way. Author Gena D. Lutz writes like a seasoned writer. In my opinion this debut novel rocks! She builds her characters up really nicely and paints a picture in your head to give you just enough for your imagination to play along with her words. She writes descriptive scenes that take you right into the battle. It's awesome! I was in the mood for a vampire, werewolf book with some new ideas brought to the table and Gena D. Lutz delivered! Thank you for an entertaining read! I can't wait for the sequel!<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText16162882950061164053" style="display:none">Thank you to The Book Avenue for hosting this tour and inviting me to join, I am very great full and excited to take part.<br /><br />We start the book by Meeting Ember and let me tell you she is a girl after my own heart; she is dominant and powerful alpha female with a literal kick ass approach and a take no crap attitude. She also happens to be a hybrid werewolf/vampire that has been around for a century or two. <br /><br />We begin to learn that Ember and her family where put under a curse by a witch a few hundred years ago, so now she will only know love when it is with her true 'heart-mate' sure she can still get her thrills with the opposite sex but she has become a true love them and leave them kind of girl. <br /><br />After her flatmate is attacked her friend Nathan calls in help from his cousin; Enter Collin. From the moment Ember set's her eyes on Collin that is it . . . she is his and he is her's . . . together forever. There hearts literally connect, and for the first time she knows what love feels like and what it is like to have a mate, or be an 'Old Lady' as her friend puts it. <br /><br />Now it is up to Ember, Collin and a few of their friends to figure out what is going on with the attacks and who they are targeting and why. Let's just keep out fingers crossed that no one gets killed in the process. <br /><br />This book is full of action, adventure and a little sexy time thrown in for good measure and trust me it is good measure I would totally like to heart mate with Collin right about now. Anyone know a single paranormal creature they can set me up with? Because I think it is safe to say that no normal man will suffice.<br /><br />Personally this book was right up my Book Avenue (Yes Cris I thought of you as a write that) I love paranormal books, they are an addiction of mine and this books ticked all the right boxes for me.<br /><br />4/5 stars.</span>

  <span id="freeText14432083038101441255" style="display:none">Emberâ€™s Curse<br />By Gena D. Lutz<br /><br />A book filled with mystery, romance and shiftersâ€¦the perfect mix of all three. <br /><br />Book Blurb: For Prime-Werewolf Ember Stilwell, life has been far from normal. Decades ago, a vengeful Witch cursed her Pack, leaving the women of her line incapable of feeling love. When an organized group of immortal killers begin to stalk and capture wolves from her pack, she sets out on a path fraught with danger. Just when it seems the world as she knows it will be changed forever, she meets Collin, an Alpha Werewolf with a body built for sin. As her heart begins to heal, she comes to find that the demons of her past are not nearly as dangerous as the nightmares she will be forced to face in her future. Can finding her true love conquer all? Or will the ability to feel for the first time be overshadowed by losing everything else she holds dear?<br /><br />I discovered this book recently as a free Amazon purchase, I often download free books without ever reading them or giving them a chanceâ€¦but I am so glad I did with this book! Ember is a fantastic character; strong, smart and full of goodness and energy. She has an alpha spirit but has followed her pack alphas direction with little question, until deaths start to happen and she starts to discover the truth. In walks Collin, What can I say about Collin? He is the perfect Alpha Male character; he is possessive, strong and spicy hot! Collin changes Embers existence; her life will never be the same but is it for the betterâ€¦or worse? <br /><br />While the characters are strong and appealing the plot was extremely enticing! I could not put the book down, I found myself reading faster and faster, learning the truth as the story unfolded and finding myself sad when the book came to an end. There is so much more to be told of Ember and Collin and many more characters to explore, I canâ€™t wait to take this ride with a new Favorite author. <span id="freeTextContainer1526641522626906599">At first I was thoroughly perturbed by the sudden relationship between the protagonist of the story and her mate. Then the author goes ahead and explains how it is possible and all is right in the (book) world again. I do like that the author accounted for almost everything; definitely ties up loose ends and answers all the questions. That said, I was confused about how the bonding tattoos work; I thought Ember and Collin received them because of her prime wolf/curse thing, but later another cou</span>
  <span id="freeText1526641522626906599" style="display:none">At first I was thoroughly perturbed by the sudden relationship between the protagonist of the story and her mate. Then the author goes ahead and explains how it is possible and all is right in the (book) world again. I do like that the author accounted for almost everything; definitely ties up loose ends and answers all the questions. That said, I was confused about how the bonding tattoos work; I thought Ember and Collin received them because of her prime wolf/curse thing, but later another couple receives them...is it just a wolf thing in general?<br /><br />Anyhow, everyone in this book sounds pretty darn attractive which seems a tad unrealistic. Then again, they are supernatural beings with crazy long life-spans, so who knows?<br /><br />Overall, a good story with a decent pace. Some romance/sex (the latter was a bit unexpected...guess I didn't read the description well?), mystery, fighting/guns/violence, vampires, wolves, and some other mystical beings (don't want to give anything away). Interested in reading the next book, to see where the author takes the story; the ending of this book seemed to tie things up nicely as is.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2173004844450471851"><strong>Enthralling!!</strong><br/><br/>I received a complimentary copy of this book for an honest review.<br/>Member's Curse has a unique spin to the paranormal world that will have you enthralled in finding out what happens next. It started out a little slow but soon heated up into an intriguing story filled with love, drama, action, friendship, and some pretty steamy encounters.<br/>Ember is a new breed of werewolves/vampire hybrid. She is a strong female character and becomes even stronger when she meets her heartmate, Collin. </span>
  <span id="freeText2173004844450471851" style="display:none"><strong>Enthralling!!</strong><br /><br />I received a complimentary copy of this book for an honest review.<br />Member's Curse has a unique spin to the paranormal world that will have you enthralled in finding out what happens next. It started out a little slow but soon heated up into an intriguing story filled with love, drama, action, friendship, and some pretty steamy encounters.<br />Ember is a new breed of werewolves/vampire hybrid. She is a strong female character and becomes even stronger when she meets her heartmate, Collin. Alpha of his own pack, Collin is the hot cousin of one of her best friends and pack-mates, Nathan. When some trouble occurs, Nathan calls Collin in to come help. They face some suspenseful and action filled situations.<br />Gena did amazing job with this paranormal romance filled with interesting characters that are werewolves, vampires, hybrids, nymphs, and a few other creatures. Along with Ember,Collin, and Nathan; she will introduce you to Harper, Milo, Teague, Roxanne, and many more wonderful characters. I can not wait to see what happens next with this series and group.</span>

  <span id="freeText10447160216358765732" style="display:none">I have a fascination with Vampires and Wolves and anything like that, so of course I jumped at the chance to read this book. The plot takes you on a journey of twists and turns with plenty of excitement mixed in through out. <br /><br />The main character Ember is easy to love with her quick wit and toughness and also her feistiness. Long ago her pack was cursed with not being able to feel love unless it was the one and only true love. Not a wonderful way to live but she makes due and it turns out all for the best. <br /><br />This book reminded me of the Anita Blake series with the wolves and vampires. I thought it was going to take the same tone as those but I was greatly surprised that it was a story all of it's own. I recommend this book if you really like vampires and wolves. It was a wonderful read. </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KzGevb63jxcQi7ytoIp/4zWoUZeD+dMzT54N9k9bX8hjaeUWnqXR30Gwi4W6+XhrBOopDL8wlzCD0Au1Z3L3cA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('x2p73ttu8NUeDrLdKUVdhf/6AoN3raeDbMBquSrm8jePMgB1+3yuHU81hfUzNloNzrh6GEtk44Cgjmz6As9ajw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
